<body style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif" bgcolor="#ffffff" text="#000000">
<div>
<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000">Exhibit 1.01<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><br>
</font></font><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 18pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #1f497d; TEXT-ALIGN: center">General Electric Company</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt"><img style="HEIGHT: 81px; WIDTH: 81px" src="image0.jpg"></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 18pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #1f497d; TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN-TOP: 6pt">2014 Conflict Minerals Report</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 18pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #1f497d; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">Introduction</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">General Electric Company ("GE" or the "Company") has prepared this Report for the year ended December 31, 2014 to satisfy the requirements of Rule 13p-1 of the Securities Exchange Act.&#160;&#160;GE manufactures a wide range of products that contain tin, tantalum, tungsten or gold ("3TG" or "Conflict Minerals"), but GE does not purchase ore or unrefined Conflict Minerals from mines and generally is many steps removed in the supply chain from the mining of these minerals.&#160;&#160;We purchase materials from a wide network of suppliers so we necessarily rely on them to assist with our reasonable country of origin inquiry.&#160;&#160;After performing a reasonable country of origin inquiry and due diligence for 2014, we have not been able to establish the conflict status of our products, due to the continued unavailability of complete information across our broad and deep supply chain.&#160; However, in 2014, the number of smelters and refiners in our supply chain that have been verified to be conflict-free substantially increased in comparison to 2013, as described under "Continuous improvement" below.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">This Report describes:</div>

<div>
<table id="d5875cc26b4a4d7798e6b38e3dcb01d5" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 54pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">&#61623;</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">the due diligence we performed for 2014, including the steps we took to mitigate the risk that Conflict Minerals in our products benefit armed groups;</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<table id="8acf3d858d6f4fb2b4fa877697940a95" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 54pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">&#61623;</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">the products that we have reason to believe might contain 3TG originating from the Democratic Republic of the Congo or an adjoining country (collectively, the "Covered Countries");</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<table id="f037a9502ca645db9878a610c89e7117" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 54pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">&#61623;</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">information known about the facilities and countries of origin of the 3TG in those products;</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<table id="1c228116241645e3a0c422aa8ae040f0" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">

</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">acronyms used in this Report; and</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<table id="2a9b6f29139b416fa4b9a8506f22b923" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 54pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">&#61623;</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">where you can find additional information about our Conflict Minerals program.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 18pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #1f497d; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt">Due Diligence</div>

<div>
<table id="ee89f62555d14c0e815e92a0ea5c0351" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; COLOR: #000000; align: right">
<div style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">1.</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">Design of GE's due diligence measures</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">GE has adopted Conflict Minerals Guidelines (the "Guidelines") that lay out the design of its Conflict Minerals due diligence process.&#160; The Guidelines describe procedures that each GE business is expected to use to perform due diligence on the source and origin of 3TG contained in products it manufactures. GE management designed our due diligence measures to conform in material respects to the<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic"> OECD Guidance for Responsible Supply Chains of Minerals from Conflict-Affected and High-Risk Areas </font>(the "OECD Guidance")<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic">, </font>the <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic">Supplement on Tin, Tantalum, and Tungsten</font> (the "Supplement"), and the <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic">Supplement on Gold</font>.</div>

<div id="DSPFPageBreakArea" style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 10pt; CLEAR: both; MARGIN-TOP: 10pt">
<div id="DSPFPageNumberArea" style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: center">5</div>

<hr id="DSPFPageBreak" style="BORDER-LEFT-WIDTH: 0px; HEIGHT: 2px; BORDER-RIGHT-WIDTH: 0px; WIDTH: 100%; BORDER-BOTTOM-WIDTH: 0px; PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; COLOR: #000000; CLEAR: both; MARGIN: 4px 0px; BORDER-TOP-WIDTH: 0px; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #000000" noshade="noshade">
</div>

<div>
<table id="34ab3379e1b04789a443a0c8ce4ccabc" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">2.</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">Description of GE's due diligence measures for 2014</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">This description of due diligence measures refers to measures performed at the GE corporate level and by the following GE businesses:&#160; Appliances &amp; Lighting, Aviation, Energy Management, Healthcare, Oil &amp; Gas, Power &amp; Water and Transportation. This description is presented pursuant to the organizational structure of the Five-Step Framework for Risk-Based Due Diligence in the Mineral Supply Chain contained in the OECD Guidance, as elaborated for downstream companies in the Supplement<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic">.</font></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #1f497d; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">Step <strong style="COLOR: #1f497d">1: &#160;</strong></font><font style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Establish strong company </font>management systems</font></div>

<div>
<table id="e8b8991650f94632bd8f51d60e8cd836" class="DSPFListTable" style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">A.</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">Adopt and commit to a supply chain policy for minerals originating from conflict-affected and high-risk areas</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">The Guidelines contain the operative provisions of GE's Statement on Conflict Minerals, which can be found on GE's website (see "Additional Resources" below), as well as the process for ensuring that risks are adequately managed.&#160; GE Corporate created and disseminated the Guidelines to each GE business for execution of GE's Conflict Minerals due diligence process.&#160; Additional GE policies that relate to the due diligence measures contained in the OECD Guidance<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic">&#160;</font>are incorporated into GE's policy document <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic">The Spirit &amp; the Letter</font>, which can be found on GE's website (see "Additional Resources" below).</div>

<div>
<table id="c32ba125b505428c9937d9f31e1ac3a5" class="DSPFListTable" style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">B.</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">Structure internal management systems to support supply chain due diligence</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">GE corporate</font>.&#160; A senior GE executive, supported by a senior GE lawyer, has oversight responsibility for GE's Statement on Conflict Minerals, including the establishment of processes and procedures to carry out this statement.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">GE businesses</font>. Each GE business has:</div>

<div>
<table id="30a8029cd9a04a889165c86352cb118f" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">&#61623;</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">established a system to support performance of due diligence on its supply chain;</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<table id="cf69a8f6d4a24bdca69f84fcb08d0661" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">

</td>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">documented that system in a written business program; and</div>
</td>

</table>
</div>

<div>
<table id="8f27f8d9b6034eaf84d931cc71f4e2ed" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">&#61623;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Internal reporting</font>.&#160; For 2014, GE Corporate used the following Conflict Minerals due diligence reporting mechanisms:</div>

<div>
<table id="1269033586f34823be0e199cfd3c373a" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">

<div>
<table id="a3644678a13345c59f221f8f53c13289" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">

</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">

</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<table id="189f86a27fce4db5be6f8543bcd105f0" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">

<div id="DSPFPageBreakArea" style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 10pt; CLEAR: both; MARGIN-TOP: 10pt">
<div id="DSPFPageNumberArea" style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: center">6</div>

<hr id="DSPFPageBreak" style="BORDER-LEFT-WIDTH: 0px; HEIGHT: 2px; BORDER-RIGHT-WIDTH: 0px; WIDTH: 100%; BORDER-BOTTOM-WIDTH: 0px; PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; COLOR: #000000; CLEAR: both; MARGIN: 4px 0px; BORDER-TOP-WIDTH: 0px; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #000000" noshade="noshade">
</div>

<div>
<table id="aa2fff97919141f4bc187dd4d4dad6d2" class="DSPFListTable" style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">C.</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">Establish a system of controls and transparency over the mineral supply chain</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Identifying suppliers</font>.&#160; Each GE business identified:</div>

<div>
<table id="f829ca3a1b874255866f5abc1ab5727e" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 54pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">&#61623;</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Relevant Suppliers:</font> suppliers that provide inputs to GE products that are known or are likely to contain 3TG through a process that is based on an examination of internal records such as bills of material or other product specifications, a qualitative review of sourcing records, or information provided by the supplier; and</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<table id="2d315b42711b4f12b668819f98264517" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 54pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">&#61623;</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Significant Suppliers:</font> those suppliers within the universe of Relevant Suppliers that are most significant to GE's Conflict Minerals program using criteria developed by the business, such as the amount of sourcing spend with the supplier.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Identifying smelters and refiners in the supply chain</font>.&#160; Each GE business identified all smelters and refiners of Conflict Minerals that are first-tier suppliers to GE and used its best efforts to collect relevant data from Significant Suppliers using a survey tool developed by GE based on the Conflict-Free Sourcing Initiative's ("CFSI") Conflict Minerals Reporting Template ("CMRT").&#160; The survey tool is designed to collect, manage and archive (for at least five years) supplier information relevant for Conflict Minerals due diligence including, among other things, the identity of smelters and refiners of 3TG in the supplier's supply chain.&#160; For 2014, GE sought to improve the quality of survey results by applying standardized criteria, based on the CMRT, for assessing the acceptability of survey responses.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Conducting a reasonable country of origin inquiry</font>.&#160; For upstream due diligence to identify countries of origin and other relevant information concerning the conflict status of metals produced by the smelters and refiners identified in GE's supply chain, GE relies on the information made available through the Conflict-Free Smelter Program ("CFSP") administered by CFSI.&#160; GE relied on this information to identify (1)&#160;the conflict status of 3TG processed by these smelters and refiners; and (2)&#160;the countries of origin of ores in the supply chains of these smelters and refiners that were listed by the CFSP as having been verified to be conflict-free during 2014.&#160;&#160;Where the CFSP data showed that ores utilized by one or more of these smelters or refiners originated in one or more of the Covered Countries, GE concluded that there is reason to believe that 3TG from the Covered Countries is present in the products of the business in the supply chain for which such smelters or refiners were reported.&#160;&#160;Due to business confidentiality and other competitive concerns, as recognized by the Supplement<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic">, </font>the CFSP does not publish detailed information on specific mine and location of origin of ores that feed the smelters and refiners subject to verification reviews.&#160; Consequently, no such information is provided in this Report.&#160;&#160;CFSP's efforts to determine such information is described on the CFSI website (see "Additional Resources" below).</div>

<div>
<table id="83d07575ee0a4b2691c1be1ee70c84f7" class="DSPFListTable" style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">D.</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">Strengthen company engagement with suppliers</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Regular communications</font>. GE regularly communicated its expectations on responsible supply chains of Conflict Minerals by transmitting surveys and other communications from the sourcing organizations of the GE businesses to Significant Suppliers and other Relevant Suppliers using an electronic survey tool.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Contractual obligations</font>. Each GE business contractually obligated Relevant Suppliers to (1)&#160;adopt policies and establish systems to use best efforts to procure Conflict Minerals from sources that have been verified as conflict free; (2)&#160;provide supporting data on their 3TG supply chains to GE when requested; and (3)&#160;provide GE with the rights to audit and terminate the contract in the event of material non-compliance.&#160; These obligations are reflected in GE's <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic">Integrity Guide for Suppliers, Contractors and Consultants </font>("Integrity Guide"), which can be found on GE's website (see "Additional Resources" below).&#160; Purchase order and contract terms and conditions in use by GE businesses bind suppliers to conform their behavior to the Integrity Guide<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic">.</font></div>

<div>
<table id="c328a3767c244ea5b11f30f1187bdc25" class="DSPFListTable" style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">E.</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">Establish a company level grievance mechanism</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Integrity Guide</font>.&#160; The Integrity Guide provides four separate methods for suppliers and supplier personnel to raise concerns about matters that are subject to the Integrity Guide, including GE's expectations of suppliers concerning Conflict Minerals.</div>

<div id="DSPFPageBreakArea" style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 10pt; CLEAR: both; MARGIN-TOP: 10pt">
<div id="DSPFPageNumberArea" style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: center">7</div>

<hr id="DSPFPageBreak" style="BORDER-LEFT-WIDTH: 0px; HEIGHT: 2px; BORDER-RIGHT-WIDTH: 0px; WIDTH: 100%; BORDER-BOTTOM-WIDTH: 0px; PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; COLOR: #000000; CLEAR: both; MARGIN: 4px 0px; BORDER-TOP-WIDTH: 0px; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #000000" noshade="noshade">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Open reporting system</font>.&#160; Each GE business also has an open reporting system through which employees and third parties may report concerns about policy violations, including concerns related to our Conflict Minerals policies. Concerns can be reported anonymously or for attribution through several channels, including the employee's manager, GE's legal department, or the relevant GE compliance officer, by calling the GE integrity hotline, or by emailing the GE Ombudsman.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">No retaliation</font>.&#160; Both the Integrity Guide and the open reporting system forbid retaliation against any person reporting an integrity concern.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #1f497d">Step 2:</font>&#160;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #1f497d">&#160;Identify and assess supply chain risks</font></div>

<div>
<table id="ff6dfe869f1640c1a78c4e0a57355a8c" class="DSPFListTable" style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">A.</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">Use best efforts to identify the smelters and refiners in the supply chain</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">During 2014, using the processes described above under "Establish a system of controls and transparency over the mineral supply chain," GE businesses identified 8,947 Relevant Suppliers (down from 9,874 in 2013), including 2,347 Significant Suppliers (down from 3,191 in 2013).&#160; Significant Suppliers identified 258 smelters and refiners of 3TG in their supply chains (up from 203 in 2013).&#160; See Table A below for a complete list of identified smelters and refiners and their validation status under the CFSI CFSP.</div>

<div>
<table id="54b25e3c23544c03825e56e6fde59052" class="DSPFListTable" style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">B.</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">Identify the scope of the risk assessment of the mineral supply chain</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Engaging with suppliers</font>.&#160; GE's Conflict Minerals supplier survey asked suppliers to identify smelters or refiners from which they made direct purchases of products containing 3TG (first-tier smelters or refiners to our first-tier suppliers), and during 2014, a number of GE suppliers reported the identities of first-tier smelters or refiners in their supply chains.&#160; In 2014, GE continued to communicate to these suppliers encouraging them to impose requirements on their first-tier smelters and refiners consistent with those that GE imposes on its first-tier suppliers, as described under "Devise and adopt a risk management plan" below.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Engaging with smelters and refiners</font>.&#160; In addition to engaging with smelters and refiners through the CFSP, GE engaged independently with tungsten smelters from which GE Lighting buys tungsten-bearing products directly ("first-tier tungsten smelters") to encourage them to participate in the smelter validation process of the CFSP.&#160; See "Devise and adopt a risk management plan" below for additional information on this engagement.</div>

<div>
<table id="4ce74b9360bc49c2b7954294b03184e9" class="DSPFListTable" style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">C.</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">Assess whether the smelters and refiners have carried out all elements of due diligence for responsible supply chains of minerals from conflict-affected and high-risk areas</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Each GE business conducted due diligence to determine the degree of compliance by suppliers with the contractual obligations laid out in the Guidelines and the accuracy of reported information based on a risk analysis and with separate levels of intensity that depend upon risk of non-compliance.&#160; Measures may include reviewing supplier responses for completeness, accuracy and credibility, and confirming smelter status by checking against the CFSI's Conflict Free Smelter list or other list of smelters that have been verified in accordance with OECD Guidance.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Lower-tier (upstream) suppliers</font>.&#160; In accordance with OECD Guidance, including its audit recommendations for downstream companies, GE implemented upstream audits by participating in and cooperating with industry organizations.&#160; GE is a partner company of CFSI and has, periodically, supported CFSI and CFSP through membership on governance committees and providing financial assistance and in-kind assistance with CFSP smelter validation.&#160; As such, GE relied on the CFSP to conduct risk assessment at the upstream level.&#160; For each smelter identified in its supply chain at the first or lower tiers, each GE business assessed the information available from the CFSP (or other audits conducted in accordance with OECD Guidance) to determine whether there were any "red flags" (as defined in OECD Guidance).</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #1f497d">Step 3:</font>&#160;&#160;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #1f497d">Design and implement a strategy to respond to identified risks</font></div>

<div>
<table id="c4aea7e3844040229c7a3011df7fd664" class="DSPFListTable" style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">

<td style="WIDTH: 72pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">A.</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">Report findings to designated senior management</div>
</td>

<div>
<table id="244b1b2bc1e64712aa7708ed25a3b53e" class="DSPFListTable" style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">

<td style="WIDTH: 72pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">B.</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">Devise and adopt a risk management plan</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Across GE</font>.&#160; Each GE business periodically compiles a report of Conflict Minerals risks identified in its supply chain at both the downstream and upstream levels for review by the GE business executive-level program owner to determine appropriate steps to take in mitigating any risks identified in the reports.&#160; In 2014, these steps focused on reducing risk by engaging those first-tier suppliers that reported purchases directly from smelters or refiners to encourage those smelters or refiners (GE's second-tier smelters or refiners) to maintain programs to eliminate from their supply chains minerals from conflict mines and become verified as conflict-free under the CFSP or a similar program.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">GE Lighting</font>.&#160; As noted above, GE Lighting has first-tier tungsten smelters in its supply chain, and, building on engagement with these smelters begun by GE Lighting as early as 2009, GE Lighting and GE Corporate in 2014 participated with the CFSP in meetings with representatives of the tungsten smelter industry to encourage tungsten smelter participation in the CFSP.&#160; Currently, 100% of the first-tier tungsten smelters that provided product to GE Lighting North America in 2014 have been verified as conflict-free under the CFSP or are scheduled for a CFSP audit, and GE Lighting has suspended purchases from first-tier tungsten smelters that are not verified or scheduled for a verification audit.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #1f497d">Step 4:</font>&#160;&#160;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #1f497d">Carry out independent 3<sup style="vertical-align: text-top; line-height: 1; font-size: smaller;">rd</sup>-party audit of smelters/refiners' due diligence practices</font></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">See "Where necessary, carry out joint spot checks at the mineral smelter or refiner's own facilities (including through participation in industry-driven programs)" above for a discussion of how GE conducted risk assessment at the upstream level.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #1f497d">Step 5:</font>&#160;&#160;&#160;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #1f497d">Report annually on supply chain due diligence</font></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">In addition to filing this Report, GE's Sustainability Report contains descriptions of its Conflict Minerals program, including a discussion of our due diligence process and progress in accomplishing the goals of our Statement on Conflict Minerals (see "Additional Resources" below).</div>

<div id="DSPFPageNumberArea" style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: center">9</div>

<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">due diligence</font> to improve the transparency in its Conflict Minerals supply chain, increasing the number of identified 3TG smelters and refiners in its supply chain by 27% to 258 in 2014; and</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<table id="38b0bafaf2b24238ac6b8fa359d21917" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 54pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">&#61623;</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">supplier engagement</font> to reduce Conflict Minerals supply chain risk, increasing the number of smelters and refiners in our supply chain that have been verified to be conflict-free by 93% to 137 in 2014.&#160; As a result, more than 50% of the smelters and refiners in our supply chain have been verified to be conflict-free.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">2015 actions to improve due diligence and supplier engagement</font>.&#160; GE intends to take the following steps in 2015 to improve due diligence and thereby mitigate the risk that Conflict Minerals in GE products may benefit armed groups:</div>

<div>
<table id="cbe231a31eb146a6aec9d7eea2f4e891" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 54pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">&#61623;</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">endeavor to continue to improve the percentage of Significant Suppliers responding to GE's supply chain surveys and the quality of their responses, by intensifying communication with suppliers and spreading across the GE businesses best practices learned during execution of the due diligence process in 2014; and</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<table id="7d105d132c4d400ead1a8d2034d9e541" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 54pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; align: right">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">&#61623;</div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">intensify the identification of and communication with GE's second-tier smelters and refiners &#8211; that is, those smelters and refiners that sell 3TG directly to GE's first-tier suppliers &#8211; in order to continue to increase the number of smelters and refiners that participate in the CFSP.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 18pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #1f497d; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt">Information Known to GE about 3TG in GE products</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">GE manufactures a wide range of products that contain Conflict Minerals, but GE does not purchase ore or unrefined conflict minerals from mines and generally is many steps removed in the supply chain from the mining of these minerals.&#160; We purchase materials from a wide network of suppliers so we necessarily rely on them to assist with our reasonable country of origin inquiry.&#160;&#160;After performing a reasonable country of origin inquiry and due diligence for 2014, we have not been able to establish the conflict status of our products, due to the continued unavailability of complete information across our broad and deep supply chain.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">Facilities Used to Process 3TG in GE Products</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">GE obtained information about the facilities used to process 3TG in GE products through the downstream due diligence activities described in this Report.&#160; <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><u>Table A</u></font> below contains a list of smelters and refiners that GE suppliers identified as being present in their supply chains that GE believes may have processed 3TG contained in GE products.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">GE obtained information about the country of origin and mine or location of origin of 3TG in GE products through reliance on the CFSP's upstream audits of smelters and refiners in GE's supply chain described in this Report.&#160; <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><u>Table B</u></font> below contains a list of known countries of origin of 3TG used by smelters and refiners that GE suppliers identified as being present in their supply chains.</div>
